< Review>
Ah, Specialty's. I've been coming here for over a year now. Here is an honest synopsis.

The Good
- The wait staff are usually friendly
- This is one of the few (if not only) place in the Bayshore Technology Park for food.
- The cookies (when done right) are to die for. Salads mostly yummy.

The Bad
- Overpriced, they have a monopoly and they know it. They have a buy 12 get 1 free deal but beware they count online and in person orders (even if you use the same card) differently.
- They have a tendency to get orders wrong or forget what you ordered even with the high tech system they have. Seriously?! But, their saving grace is amazing customer service, they will fix what they do wrong if you complain, as well give you free stuff on your next visit -- decent.
- They often burn cookies, I don't know why.
- Just about every sandwich here is made with gobs of cream cheese. The breakfast sandwiches are dry and skimpy on the meat. Why not compete with other places nearby by offering them on bagels, English muffins, or in the form of a breakfast burrito? It wouldn't be a stretch.
- Worst thing is the paper cups they use for coffee. They are good for one use. If you refill it, the stuff the paper is made out of leaches into your drink and tastes like you are eating rotten painted cardboard, yech.

There are 3 starbucks and a peet's nearby, so I'd recommend getting coffee elsewhere, but if you have a hunger for the other good stuff they are known for, Specialty's aims to please.<//Review>

< Text>
This a great place to come for a walk to get away from urban sprawl. The Arroyo Seco cuts through the western part of Pasadena and provides a natural area of trees and wildlife providing you can ignore the concrete channel containing the mostly dry Arroyo Seco Creek. From the Colorado Street Bridge south to the Los Angeles River, there are easy pathways and plenty of places to explore.< /Text>

< Review>
Unless you have a specific purpose to be here, this park is one you should skip. It‚Äôs permit parking only with a single road in and out up and down a hill with low visibility. Getting out and walking is ok, but you‚Äôre in a valley and miss so much of the beautiful area around you.</Review>

<Gmap_id>0x80c2c39b05ab82ed:0x6f0a1d1f400d2c5a</Gmap_id><Pictures>None< /Pictures>< Review>
I come here as a Member of the Roving Archers Group. Great variation of different outdoor Archery Targets to shoot at. I believe there are people who come out there to shoot who have either not purchased the membership card as they come out playing music and talking super loud. There is nothing worse than trying to concentrate on the target when people in the lane next to you are blaring their music. I suggest contacting The Pasadena Roving Archers and paying the $20 to take the Safety and Certification class. You get a membership card and 2 years unlimited access to more than 20 Outdoor Targets to shoot at, no Broadhead Arrows!<//Review>

< text>
Arroyo Seco Trail is a 4 mile (round trip)  loop trail located near Pasadena, California and is good for all skill levels. The trail is good for hiking, walking, and trail running. It has an easy flat trail with no elevation. The trail start at the San Pascual stables in South Pasadena and ends by the Colorado street bridge. There are no major scenic view except for the bridge and the canal. However, this trail is good to get a cardio-workout. Overall, it's a decent trail with lots of trees and shrubs.<//text>

< review>
Great for jogging, strolling, or walking your dog! Follow the Arroyo river downstream for miles. Look for the hidden benches and grass area that are perfect for a picnic. Also, going north is worth: go under the Pasadena bridge and follow the river to the Rose Bowl (~30-45min).<//review>

I unfortunately had a terrible experience with this post office at two different instances. The first situation occurred when I waited at home for a package that was guaranteed to arrive by 12:00 on a given day and actually arrived at 4 pm. This usually wouldn't be a problem, but the post person dishonestly reported that the package was delivered at 11:15, so the money was not refundable - and it was incredibly time sensitive. Not to mention that I ended up having to take off work because the package was late.

The second instance is even worse. I waited at home again one day to receive a guaranteed priority package. The post person delivered one of my packages, but not the second priority package. They did, however, mark that the package had been delivered, which I know was not true because I was sitting outside when the other package was delivered. I went to the post office two days later (arriving an hour early to make sure I would be able to talk to someone as soon as it opened), and the person behind the counter raised their voice telling me the package hadn't been delivered yet and that I needed to be patient. When he took a deep breath and looked at the tracking information he realized he had read the information incorrectly. Rather than apologize he said, let me get my supervisor. He returned several minutes later saying his supervisor wouldn't talk to me until 9 pm (which didn't work for an individual with work).

I filed a report and attempted to call the post office numerous times, only to be put on hold for hours or not answered. So incredibly frustrating. Especially because I have used USPS for years and never experienced this before. The report I filed was later changed to "Resolved" even though I was not contacted or explained how...

The package is gone, and I will likely never find it.</text>

Dr. Banooni was negligent with me.  TWICE.  He unnecessarily caused me enormous pain, left me to languish in it and showed not an ounce of sympathy or concern when I let him know I was in pain over two months ago.  But that wasn't his first negligent action...

I ended up with migraines within days, and they changed it a week later.  However, I was not given any explanation, or apology.  Just a rather condescending response, "I guess you know your own body."  Um, yeah, I'm not a doctor, nor some anti-vaxxing, anti-science freak, but I am medically informed.  I also expect that if we agree on inserting a SKYLA IUD because of my history of high estrogen and progesterone, I would hope I would wake up with a SKYLA inside me!  Seems reasonable, right?  But he was so well "respected" so I chalked it up to an honest mistake and let it go.  That was my mistake.  I should have left then and there.

I also had a history of fibroids, which I made sure to mention that they be monitored carefully since I already had a myomectomy at the age of 36 to remove several large fibroids.  Bottom line, even though Banooni had 3 ultrasounds over 3 years to look at, he treated me like a whiner when I sent him an ultrasound ordered by my Internist in Feb and complained of  pain 3 weeks out of the month of my cycle.  Banooni had no urgency to see me and put me off a month to even examine me!!!   I asked him politely to see me sooner since I was in pain and exhausted all the time.

My potential surgery to relieve me of my now worsening pain, got postponed indefinitely.  Meanwhile my belly had grown to the size of a 6 month pregnancy and my back was so painful I couldn't walk! What sets him apart from though from other doctor in this specialty is his COMPASSION-he is truly compassionate in every way: when you first meet him as a new patient you will feel at ease immediately due to his GENTLE, kind, warm, thoughtful manner. and his understanding.  He is incredibly understanding in every way-and he cares for me as a whole person-SO incredibly important- His compassion, gentleness, and understanding is evident in EVERY way he cares for you as a patient. You'll feel it the way he takes the time to fully and deeply hear and address each of your thoughts and concerns, and really every way in which he cares for you as a doctor! I have additional medical issues, having had three surgeries on my spine, and Dr. Banooni's wonderful care of all of the secondary issues that stem from that, and the way he works with my entire team of doctors-and always has is so amazing too...In addition, Dr. Banooni's STAFF are also incredible! They are very kind, thoughtful and compassionate to me. I feel that is VERY important. The office is located on the 2nd floor of a beautiful Medical Plaza, and  the waiting room is very serene, private and comfortable-the inner area where Dr. Banooni's office and the examination rooms are located is very comfortable as well. In so many words, Dr. Banooni is the epitome of what an Ob/Gyn should be in every single way, and I am always very happy to recommend him wholeheartedly!< /review>
